Computing effective sample size using the LDSC method:
 Neff = (N_CAS+N_CON) * (N_CAS/(N_CAS+N_CON)) / mean((N_CAS/(N_CAS+N_CON))[(N_CAS+N_CON)==max(N_CAS+N_CON)]))
